# Pair (starter ‚Üê‚Üí starter + nonstarter) (322)

### `U+00C0` [0] ‚Äî LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH GRAVE

**Decomposition:** ‚Üí `U+0041` [0] + `U+0300` [230]

**`U+0041` combines forwards with:**

- **code point** + `U+0328` [202] ‚Üí `U+0104` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH OGONEK
- **code point** + `U+0323` [220] ‚Üí `U+1EA0` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH DOT BELOW
- **code point** + `U+0325` [220] ‚Üí `U+1E00` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH RING BELOW
- **code point** + `U+0300` [230] ‚Üí `U+00C0` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH GRAVE
- **code point** + `U+0301` [230] ‚Üí `U+00C1` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH ACUTE
- **code point** + `U+0302` [230] ‚Üí `U+00C2` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH CIRCUMFLEX
- **code point** + `U+0303` [230] ‚Üí `U+00C3` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH TILDE
- **code point** + `U+0304` [230] ‚Üí `U+0100` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH MACRON
- **code point** + `U+0306` [230] ‚Üí `U+0102` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH BREVE
- **code point** + `U+0307` [230] ‚Üí `U+0226` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH DOT ABOVE
- **code point** + `U+0308` [230] ‚Üí `U+00C4` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH DIAERESIS
- **code point** + `U+0309` [230] ‚Üí `U+1EA2` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH HOOK ABOVE
- **code point** + `U+030A` [230] ‚Üí `U+00C5` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH RING ABOVE
- **code point** + `U+030C` [230] ‚Üí `U+01CD` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH CARON
- **code point** + `U+030F` [230] ‚Üí `U+0200` [0] LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH DOUBLE GRAVE
